\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} The driving force module. Provides the storage and manipulation methods.

\Hypertarget{classopenphase_1_1DrivingForce_a76f5688451ff45f805c7ff0a2523bfd9}\label{classopenphase_1_1DrivingForce_a76f5688451ff45f805c7ff0a2523bfd9} 
\index{openphase::DrivingForce@{openphase::DrivingForce}!MaxTimeStep@{MaxTimeStep}}
\index{MaxTimeStep@{MaxTimeStep}!openphase::DrivingForce@{openphase::DrivingForce}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MaxTimeStep()}{MaxTimeStep()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily double openphase\+::\+Driving\+Force\+::\+Max\+Time\+Step (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classopenphase_1_1PhaseField}{Phase\+Field}} \&}]{Phase,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classopenphase_1_1InterfaceProperties}{Interface\+Properties}} \&}]{IP,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classopenphase_1_1Settings}{Settings}} \&}]{OPSettings,  }\item[{double}]{Theor\+Limit = {\ttfamily 1.0},  }\item[{double}]{Num\+Limit = {\ttfamily 1.0e-\/3} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calculates minimum number of phase field iterations for a given time step. 

This function calculates the maximum time step for the phase field equation time integration.

This function uses two different stability criteria\+:

1) Neumann stability criterion for phase-\/field equation\+: dt \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0.\+5\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}dx\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}2/(Interface\+Energy\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+Interface\+Mobility) (Theor\+Limit is set to 1.\+0 by default); 2) Numerical criterion, where the maximum phase-\/field increment in the whole simulation domain has to be lower than 1E-\/3 (Numer\+Limit is set to 1E-\/3 by default).

If phase field gets unstable, decrease Theor\+Limit, if diffusion field becomes unstable due to too high phase-\/field increments, decrease Numer\+Limit.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{DrivingForce_8cpp_source_l00722}{722}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{DrivingForce_8cpp_source}{Driving\+Force.\+cpp}}.
